# Enable Powerlevel10k instant prompt. Should stay close to the top of ~/.zshrc.
if [[ -r "${XDG_CACHE_HOME:-$HOME/.cache}/p10k-instant-prompt-${(%):-%n}.zsh" ]]; then
  source "${XDG_CACHE_HOME:-$HOME/.cache}/p10k-instant-prompt-${(%):-%n}.zsh"
fi

# Path to your Oh My Zsh installation.
export ZSH="$HOME/.oh-my-zsh"

# Theme
ZSH_THEME="powerlevel10k/powerlevel10k"

# Plugins (una sola dichiarazione!)
plugins=(
  git
  docker
  docker-compose
  node
  npm
  python
  zsh-autosuggestions
  zsh-syntax-highlighting
  z
  history-substring-search
  colored-man-pages
  command-not-found
  sudo
)

source $ZSH/oh-my-zsh.sh

# ============================================
# PATH
# ============================================
export PATH="$PATH:/home/nuno/.turso"

# ============================================
# EDITOR
# ============================================
export VISUAL="code --wait"
export EDITOR="code --wait"

# ============================================
# ALIAS PERSONALIZZATI
# ============================================
# Color aliases (già gestiti meglio da Oh My Zsh, ma li teniamo per compatibilità)
alias ls='ls --color=auto'
alias grep='grep --color=auto'
alias fgrep='fgrep --color=auto'
alias egrep='egrep --color=auto'

# Directory listings
alias ll='ls -alF'
alias la='ls -A'
alias l='ls -CF'

# Utility
alias cls='clear'
alias alert='notify-send --urgency=low -i "$([ $? = 0 ] && echo terminal || echo error)" "$(history|tail -n1|sed -e '\''s/^\s*[0-9]\+\s*//;s/[;&|]\s*alert$//'\'')"'

# Git shortcuts
alias gs='git status'
alias gd='git diff'

# Importa alias personalizzati se esistono
if [ -f ~/.bash_aliases ]; then
  source ~/.bash_aliases
fi

# Language environment
export LANG=en_US.UTF-8

# To customize prompt, run `p10k configure` or edit ~/.p10k.zsh.
[[ ! -f ~/.p10k.zsh ]] || source ~/.p10k.zsh
# Bridge ADB verso Windows

# Rileva il file corretto e aggiunge le righe per ADB
CURRENT_RC="$HOME/.$(basename $SHELL)rc"
echo -e "\n# Bridge ADB verso Windows\nsource $CURRENT_RC

# Bridge ADB verso Windows

# --- JARVIS ALIASES E PATH ---
export PATH="$HOME/.local/bin:$PATH"

alias jarvis-start='nohup /home/nuno/.local/bin/zeroclaw -w /mnt/c/Users/Nuno/Documents/programmazione/11_JARVIS_project/jarvis_local > /home/nuno/zeroclaw.log 2>&1 &'
alias jarvis-stop='pkill zeroclaw'
alias jarvis-logs='tail -f /home/nuno/zeroclaw.log'
alias jarvis-restart='jarvis-stop 2>/dev/null; sleep 1; jarvis-start'

# --- ADB BRIDGE WINDOWS ---
export WIN_IP=$(ip route show default | awk '"'"'{print $3}'"'"')
export ADB_SERVER_SOCKET=tcp:$WIN_IP:5037
